<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic Hotel My husband  I and our daughter have just returned from spending 3 nights at this wonderful hotel. From the moment we arrived by taxi we were treated exceptionally well. As we were sharing the room they gave us a larger room which had a separate TV room with a single bed for our daughter. Our room was extremely comfortable and very clean and the bathroom was a great size. Although we didn't have a view of the Arc de Triomphe we did look out towards the roundabout which was very pleasant. Farook at the front desk was so helpful and advised us of great eateries in the area. All of the staff were friendly and spoke very good English. The location of this hotel is excellent, just a short walk to the Champs Elysees and the Arc and the RER and Metro are across the street. We took the RER to EuroDisney and had a great day. After travelling around Europe for 24 days on a coach we were delighted to find a laundromat within 5 minutes walk of the hotel - go across the street outside the hotel and walk left, take the first right and then left and the laundromat is down this street on the left (4 euros for a wash and 1 euro for 10 minutes in the dryer). We will definitely be staying at this hotel when next visiting Paris.

<Author>TomLosAngeles
<Content>Great Hotel, Great Concierge! My wife and I stayed at the hotel for a week and half in early May, 2006, and had a fantastic time. The location couldn't be better -- right across the street from the Arc de Triomph. The metro stops right in front of the hotel, a taxi stand is just across the street, and the Champs Elysees is right there. We booked a suite on the 6th floor, and I'm sure that you won't find a better view in any hotel in the city. You can pay twice as much at the Four Seasons and have no view at all, for example. Best of all about the hotel was the concierge, Farooq. He was extraordinarily helpful, and a very nice guy. He was able to get us into the top Michelin-rated restaurants, and get opera tickets as well, all on relatively short notice. But he also had great ideas and suggestions for places to go, places to eat, etc., that you probably would never find unless you were a local. We heartily recommend the hotel to everybody.

<Author>sandijen
<Content>Great Hotel My husband and I have just returned from 5 days Paris where we celebrated our first wedding anniversary. Like someone mentioned recently, I too booked the Splendid Etoile when it was number 2 in the ranks and almost changed to another hotel as I watched the ratings decline over the past few months - I needn't have worried. The service we received was polite and extremely helpful and nothing was too much trouble. The location couldn't have been more central and with a metro literally right outside we could whizz around the city in no time! There's a boulangerie at the bottom of the street where you can eat breakfast for 7 Euros per person. Their croissants au beurre are fantastic! Please do as we tried to do and make an effort to speak their language - you'll get so much more from your holiday.....French is the most romantic language in the world after all!An absolute must is a late night trip to the top of the Arc de Triomphe - there are no queues at that time and the city is just beautiful all lit up. Try to time it so that you're at the top just before the Eiffel Tower 'sparkles' (on the hour and lasts around 10-15 minutes).We love Paris and will have no hesitations about staying at the Splendid Etoile in the future.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Paris we love you! Abbotsford, BC Just returned from a week long stay in Paris and at the Splendid Etoile Hotel. Had a fantastic time!!! The Splendid Etoile was clean, comfortable and quiet. Farook at the front desk was super friendly, helpful and spoke great english. It is a great location as the Air France bus drops you off right across the street from the hotel front door, we could see the Arc de Triumph out of our window and the hop on/hop off bus has a stop just on the other side of the roundabout. Secondly, don't let people tell you Paris is soo expensive - it is as expensive as you want to make it. We would eat our breakfast along the Champs at Paul (a patisserie) 3 coissants/2 grand coffees just under 10.00 euro - sandwiches there around 5 euro each. Easy to find lunch for 9 to 11 euro each. Remeber the food quality is great for the price that you pay. The drinks of any kind are pricey. It seemed any museum was around 7.50 euro each to get in (to see Monet's, Van Gogh's, Rembrandt's, DaVinci's!!!). We found the audio guides at 5 euro each helpful (shared). We found alot of english spoken along the Champs but much less off that street. But who cares! Try your hand at the French, so what if you butcher it at least you are trying and they appreciate the effort, and it's fun! Prepare to walk alot which we found great because there is so much to see along the way that before you know it you've walked 3 miles! We are already planning our next trip!

<Author>JRChicago
<Content>Solid value, good location, nice views We booked 5 nights directly with the hotel (via e-mail) and saved about 15-20 Euro/night vs any of the web sites including the hotel site. The location is very good, there is a major Metro and RER stop directly outside the hotel which makes travel all around Paris a breeze. Note the importance of this being a major metro stop which serves multiple lines, not all stops have this convenience. Would recommend taking the Air France bus from CDG as the bus make only two stops and one is directly at the hotel. The rooms were nice, but nothing out of the ordinary. Confortable, quiet, clean, reasonable size, helpful staff, but nothing beyond ordinary. Be careful with restaurant recommendations from the concierge, he has a closet full of business cards and could be getting a spiff from the places he recommends. We had much better luck using Access or one of several web sites for dinning recommendations.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A room with a view My wife, two daughters, and I stayed in Hotel Splendid Hotel for six nights. I booked it directly though the hotel by e-mail after viewing their website. I chose it primarily because of excellent reviews on Tripadvisor and largely because we had better experience, generally, in smaller hotels. In my e-mail I wrote what I was looking for and I promptly received a favorable reply from the hotel. We stayed in room 606 on the top floor with breathtaking view of the Arc de Triomphe and the Tour Eiffel. It was a beautifully appointed suite with French furniture and decor but with a pleasant minimalist feel to it. To the delight of my 9 and 11 year old daughters, the staff prepared two separate beds for them in the sitting room. The largest in the sixth floor, the room provided ample space for my family. The marble bathroom, impeccably clean and religiously supplied with generous toiletries, towels, and bathrobes, has very strong water pressure.The members of the staff especially the concierge were very cordial and polite. They provided excellent suggestions for restaurants and helpful tips on how to go about your daily trips around the city. The hotel's location couldn't be more perfect. The Metro station is right in front of the hotel.We chose not to eat any of our meals in the hotel because ther are many restaurants, brassieries, and cafes nearby that offer excellent food for better value. Two of our favourites are the Lateral, only two small blocks from the hotel, and Jacques boulangerie, about three blocks. Our dining experience have been wonderful--courteous staff and expeditious service, and of course, great food. (It is true, the French can really cook!)I will certainly stay in this hotel again on our next trip to Paris.

<Content>Good location for tourists but the hotel is ok Stayed there for two nights in March. The hotel has an excellent location. From some rooms (not all though) you will enjoy the view of the Arc. <Author>BoldlyGO
<Content>Friendly but over priced? I booked this hotel for myself, my husband and 12 year old by email and got a very friendly reply, and a triple room. The reviews on this site were helpful, but perhaps a bit American? I can see why our transatlantic cousins and business people would love the hotel - dark wood, powerful showers etc. It is in a great location as others have said. Our triple was a suite with the attached room sofa turned into a bed (room 109), and was very good and spacious with a huge bathroom! It overlooked the side street, and a minus would be not being able to have the windows open. The maid was great and funny too. The reception were charming, and the area very good. Breakfasts at the hotel were not good value for money - we recommend the jolly French famille at the Emperor opposite where you can have anything from just a croissant and coffee to their take on an English or American breakfast! Go down the road, and you are in a French neighbourhood. The French should do something about the dark dank underpass (built in the 70s?) which takes you to the Arc de Triomphe!!To sum up, a very good hotel, but a little pricey, probably because of the location. We are glad we went though as the Metro is just outside the door and our son loved the little lift down!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A pleasant surprise We decided on this hotel after reading all of the reviews on this site. I read so many bad reviews on hotels in Paris my expectations were set very low for my firs Europe trip.this hotel was a nice surprise. We upgraded to the superior room for a nominal charge through travelocity. The room was of average size compared to american hotels. Pleanty of room for two. Actually enought room to spread out and excercise. the heating is very good. Too good. We opened the windows at night to cool it down at times. The shower was ok with the pressure and temp. It had a shower curtain which i guess is rare. the windows are all french style doors that open to walk out onto the balcony and are double paned which made them almost sound proof except for a few sirens or scooter sounds that would get through.The staff is great. Spoke very good english and always started with the language they knew their guest spoke. Our concierge spoke seven languages.We requested a room with a view of the arch d' triomphe and got one with a balcony view meaning that you could only see it from the balcony. There are only a few rooms with the view you see online. This kinda bummed us at first but turned out to not be a big deal. The lobby area is tiny with a nice little bar area. They had a daily variety of different language newspapers for free. The elevators are hilariously small, but we got a chuckle out of them everytime. We never tried the restaurant or breakfast buffet as there are numerous places in the area at much cheaper rates. They have high speed internet in the room for 14 euros for 24 hours. But there are too also many cafes with free wi-fi close by. The area couldn't be a more convienient location. The metro is just acroos the street which connects to the main line to all the sites. The metro is fantastic, easy and safe at all hours.There are so many restaurants in the area we never ventured futher than a few blocks for our dinners.I recommend if you fly into CDG to take the Air France bus. It's available to all for around 14 euros round trip. It drops you off directly in front of the hotel.Overall we were very pleased and pleasantly surprised.

<Author>gulfgirl
<Content>The perfect Paris haven My husband and I recently returned from Paris having spent 4 nights at The Splendid Etoile celebrating our silver wedding anniversary. Because it was such a special occasion and we were travelling all the way from Dubai to be there, I had researched hotels extensively on Trip Advisor before deciding on this hotel --and we were absolutely delighted with our choice ! From the moment we stepped through the door till the time we left for the airport we had friendly , courteous and prompt service. The chief concierge , M. Haroun was delightful and gave us all kinds of helpful tips. On the advice of a Trip Advisor member we had asked for room 407 which was a superior room with two balconies overlooking the Arch de Triumph. The room was exactly as we had seen on the web site and well appointed, with clean carpets and extremely comfortable beds. The bathroom was spacious and clean and had a lovely warm radiator! At night when the Arch is lit up, it looks magical through the windows with all the lights twinkling on the Champs Elysee! It was so special to wake up each morning and look out of the window and know immediately you were in Paris !!!Our room rate included the buffet breakfast which was served in a cosy little room off the lobby and we were able to start each day with a cooked meal. However, they do have a continental option with a variety of juices, cereals, fruit and breads which looked quite filling and delicious.The hotel is comveniently located on Avenue Carnot and there is an underpass that takes you to the Champs Elysee--about a 5 minute walk. There is a taxi stand by the hotel door and an RER station right in front as well. There is also a metro station a couple of minutes away. We found the taxis to be very reasonably priced and since everything we wanted to see was so close to the hotel it was easy and cheap to get to. For instance, to get to the Musee D'Orsay cost us about 5 euro by taxi. The hotel has a restaurant and a bar and we were pleasantly surprised by the quality of the food there. There are also a number of cafes and brasseries on and around Avenue Carnot which offer cheaper options. Down the road there are two alimentaries, a boulangerie and patisserie as well as a wine shop so one could also pick up bread and cheese, meats and salads for eating in or a picnic.We had a wonderful time and would love to return to the Splendid Etoile. On our previous visit to Paris we had stayed in the Latin Quarter but we enjoyed our time in the Etoile far more!  
<Date>Mar 4, 2006

<Author>LoungeLover
<Content>All you need I stayed at the Splendid for one night, looking for something central and comfortable. I have sampled a lot of hotels in Paris but this one hits the spot. As others have said before me, it is just off the Arc de Triomphe but also on the other side of the street of where the Air France bus drops you off coming from the aiport. It's a 5mn walk to the Champs Elysees, but it also has some very nice restaurants and bars just down the street and in the entire area of Avenue des Ternes.The rooms are big, the beds comfortable, the view breathtaking, the bathrooms clean and big. I got a great deal at 190Euros a night including breakfast and have to say that I will most certainly be back. It's all about location here. It's just a shame that when I was here there seemed to be some renovation work going on on the 2nd floor, so ask before they give you your room number, because this was quite annoying in the morning.Other than that (and hoping it is only temporary) this is a great choice of hotel!

<Author>Rainyuk
<Content>Lovely hotel! We鈥檝e just returned from a one-night weekend stay at the Hotel Splendid Etoile in Paris. The reception staff were friendly, spoke excellent English and couldn鈥檛 do enough to accommodate us. I booked a superior room but upon checking in (which they kindly let us do a couple of hours early) they gave us a free upgrade to a suite, which was an unexpected but very welcome bonus! I enquired at the desk about an iron and within 10 minutes an iron and ironing board were delivered to my room!On Saturday evening, we ate at the restaurant Le Pr茅 Carre attached to the hotel and my hubby, the steak connoisseur, adored his filet steak and said it was one of the best he鈥檇 eaten. I had rack of lamb, which was equally fantastic, and the profiteroles were to die for.The weather was cold and drizzly after dinner on Saturday night and we were very glad of our suite as instead of going for a walk we bought some wine and cosied up in the room by the window, overlooking the Arc de Triomphe and watching the crazy traffic and the lights twinkle on the Eiffel Tower.Tips: (1) We didn鈥檛 take breakfast at the hotel 鈥?even though it looked nice 鈥?as hubby wanted something 鈥榗ooked鈥?so we went to the caf茅 on the opposite corner and had a tasty breakfast of cheese omelette, French bread, croissant and jam, OJ and hot choc 鈥?divine 鈥?all for 鈧?1.90.(2) The bar at Planet Hollywood has a happy hour at around 4 pm (not sure if that鈥檚 every day but it applied to Sunday) 鈥?all drinks half price.(3) The mini bar is a tad expensive - you can buy beer, wine and snacks from the supermarket at the bottom of the hill for much less.I鈥檇 cannot thank the hotel enough for a lovely anniversary weekend as it was pure magic.(there was only one down side to the trip and that was the taxi ride from the hotel to station for the journey home. The hotel kindly called a taxi for us and instead of taking 10 minutes and costing 鈧?.50 as it did on the way to the hotel, it took an hour and cost over 鈧?5! We felt well and truly ripped off 鈥?a London cabbie would have tried all kinds of back street routes to get us there quickly 鈥?this guy sat on one long road just inching along! That was at 6.20 pm on a Sunday evening). Good thing we left in plenty of time!All in all, I would definitely recommend Hotel Splendid Etoile!

<Author>macjellicoe
<Content>Delighted with our choice Splendid Etoile - convenient location, courtesy, and comfort are some of the factors that influence me to wholeheartedly recommend this hotel.Thank you to all previous contributors, your information and comments helped me to decide on and select this hotel as the location to stay on our first trip to Paris.We were delighted with our choice. For us it proved to be ideal.Transferring from CdG airport using the Air France bus was easy, quick, and convenient. The bus has a stance at Avenue Carnot, and the hotel is across the road.The reception staff in the hotel, were pleasant efficient, and have fluent English.The room was a good size, clean and well looked after.Breakfast was included in our tariff, and we were satisfied with the choice available on the Continental Breakfast.With the Metro available just outside the hotel, and the open-top tourist buses available at the Arc de Triomphe (when you come out of the hotel proceed in a clockwise direction round the Arc and you will find the tourist buses) getting to and from all the major sights was easy.We will certainly use this hotel on future trips to Paris.

<Author>BERNEY56
<Content>Great for Women traveling alone! Its been quite awhile since I stayed at Splendid Etoile but from reading reviews I'm very glad to know it has not changed! This is the perfect location and setting. As a woman traveling alone for business I felt safe and very much at home at Splendid Etoile. I've longed to go back for a romantic holiday, but not that lucky yet. I have stayed in the room where you are looking at the Arch d'Triomphe gain that rosy glow in the late summer afternoons -- magnificent. I've visited Paris as well as worked there many times and I have yet to find a more convenient location. You can get to most everywhere without a transfer and find it most convenient for business and sightseeing. This is not the modern hotel with business facitlities -- its just a much more enjoyable option than staying at La Defense at a much more reasonable rate than the other business hotels in the area. Some of the most memorable memories I have is of the Splendid Etoile bathrooms and those huge lovely tubs! Hopefully they still supply the bubbling bath gel....
